**GT:** `-0.1286*sqrt(A) - 0.1286*A*exp(-0.0594*t) + 0.3894*sin(0.5829*A)`

The GT has three terms:
1. `-c*sqrt(A)` (proportional to A^0.5)
2. `-c*A*exp(-kt)` (A times decaying exponential in t)
3. `c*sin(bA)` (sine function of A)

Let me look for candidates that can produce: sqrt(A), A*exp(ct), and sin(A*c) terms.

**Candidate 23:** `c0*t*exp(c1*t) + c2*exp(c3/A) + c4*sin(A*c5 + c6*log(c7*t + 1) + c8)`

The sin term has `log(c7*t+1)` inside, which can't be eliminated (setting c6=0 removes t-dependence from sin, but then we need the A*exp term separately). The first term is `t*exp(c1*t)` which isn't `A*exp(ct)`. No match.

**Candidate 19:** `A*c0*exp(c1*t) + A^c2*c3 + A^c4*c5 + c6*t*exp(c7*t)`

Setting c2=0.5 gives `c3*sqrt(A)`, c4 could give another power of A. But we need sin(A), which isn't here. No match.

**Candidate 16:** `A*c0 + A^c1*c2 + c3*tanh(c4*t + c5) + c6*cos(A*c7 + c8*log(c9*t + 1))`

- `A*c0`: linear in A
- `A^c1*c2`: set c1=0.5 → sqrt(A) term ✓
- `c3*tanh(c4*t+c5)`: tanh, not exp. Can't produce A*exp(t).
- `c6*cos(...)`: has log(t) inside, and no A*exp term.

No A*exp(-kt) term. No match.

**Candidate 43:** `A*c0*exp(A*c1) + c2/(c3+t) + c4*exp(c5*t)*sin(A*c6 + c7)`

- `A*c0*exp(A*c1)`: set c1=0 → c0*A. Not sqrt(A).
- `c4*exp(c5*t)*sin(A*c6+c7)`: This mixes exp(t) with sin(A). The GT has sin(A) without t-dependence and A*exp(t) without sin.

This can't separate into independent sin(A) and A*exp(t) terms. No match.

**Candidate 5:** `A^5*c0*exp(c1*t) + A^2*c2*exp(c3*t) + A^c4*c5 + c6*t*exp(c7*t) + c8*exp(c9/A)`

- Set c0=0 (kill A^5 term)
- `A^2*c2*exp(c3*t)`: need A*exp, not A^2*exp. No good.
- No sin term. No match.

**Candidate 34:** `A*c0 + A*c1*t/(c2+t) + A^c3*c4 + c5*tanh(c6*t+c7)`

No sin or exp terms that match. No match.

**Candidate 1:** `A*c0 + A^c1*c2*t/(c3+t) + c4*tanh(c5*t+c6) + c7*exp(A^c8*c9)`

No sin term. No match.

Let me reconsider. The GT has sin(bA) which is quite specific. Looking through all candidates for sin terms: candidates 3, 13, 16, 23, 41, 43.

None of these candidates simultaneously have:
1. A sin(c*A) term (without t-dependence)
2. An A*exp(c*t) term
3. A sqrt(A) or A^c term

Going back through all candidates more carefully... None seem to have a pure sin(A) term combined with A*exp(t) and sqrt(A).

The closest might be candidate 23 but it lacks A*exp(t), or candidate 43 but sin and exp are multiplied together.
